The Medal will be awarded at a Ceremonial Session of the 2017 AAPT Winter Meeting, in Atlanta, Georgia.  The Oersted Medal recognizes his outstanding, widespread, and lasting impact on the teaching of physics through his contributions to the use of computer simulations to motivate active learning.</p>\n</div>\n<p class=\"readmore\"><a href=\"http://www.aapt.org/aboutaapt/pressreleases/2017_AAPT_Oersted_Jan_Tobochnik.cfm\">Read more »</a></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<h3>AAPT and Partners Awarded NSF Grant to Integrate Computation, Modeling, and Physics First</h3>\n<p class=\"date\">Sep 16 2016</p>\n<div class=\"contents\">\n<p>The National Science Foundation announced that it has awarded the American Association of Physics Teachers a nearly $1.25 million grant to help teachers effectively plan and implement classroom instruction in algebra-based Physics First courses that integrates computational thinking through two existing research-based approaches - Modeling Instruction for physics and Bootstrap for computational modeling.  Working with Physics First teachers will allow this project to impact student populations which will be demographically more diverse than students historically enrolled in standalone computer science courses or upper-grade physics courses.</p>\n</div>\n<p class=\"readmore\"><a href=\"http://aapt.org/K12/K12-Blog.cfm#15September2016&#10;\">Read more »</a></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<h3>Presidential Awards for Excellence in Mathematics and Science Teaching include AAPT Members</h3>\n<p class=\"date\">Aug 25 2016</p>\n<div class=\"contents\">\n<p>Seven AAPT members will be honored later this summer as recipients of the prestigious Presidential Award for Excellence in Mathematics and Science Teaching (PAEMST). The criterion for selection of Fellows is exceptional contribution to AAPT’s mission, to enhance the understanding and appreciation of physics through teaching. Fellowship is a distinct honor signifying recognition by one's professional peers. Any AAPT member who has maintained an active membership for at least 7 years is eligible for nomination for Fellowship. Nominations are evaluated by the AAPT Awards committee and approved by the AAPT Board of Directors.</p>\n</div>\n<p class=\"readmore\"><a href=\"http://www.aapt.org/aboutaapt/pressreleases/2016fellows.cfm&#10;\">Read more »</a></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<h3>2016 U.S. Physics Team Scores 2 Gold and 3 Silver Medals</h3>\n<p class=\"date\">Jul 18 2016</p>\n<div class=\"contents\">\n<p>Out of the ninety participating counties, the U.S. tied for 7th on the medal count, with two gold and three silver medals. In light of these discussions, the AAPT Board of Directors and Executive Office affirms that the Association expects the highest level of professional behavior of everyone at its meetings and events.  We all want AAPT meetings and workshops to be productive and welcoming for all and that means we all need to treat each other with respect and dignity.  If you experience any unethical behavior or see such behavior directed towards someone else at the meeting, you may report that behavior to one of the AAPT staff so that appropriate action can be taken.  AAPT will soon release a formal Code of Conduct and lay out the details of procedures to be followed in case violations of that Code are reported.</p>\n<p></p>\n</div>\n<p class=\"readmore\"><a href=\"http://www.aapt.org/aboutaapt/organization/code_of_conduct.cfm\">Read more »</a></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<h3>U.S. Physics Team Travelers Selected for the 2016 International Physics Olympiad</h3>\n<p class=\"date\">Jun 06 2016</p>\n<div class=\"contents\">\n<p>Five students have been selected to represent the U.S. Physics Team as the 2016 Traveling Team at the 47th International Physics Olympiad, a competition among high-school physics students, to be held July 10 –18, 2016 in Switzerland and Liechtenstein. </p>\n</div>\n<p class=\"readmore\"><a href=\"http://aapt.org/aboutaapt/pressreleases/2016physics_travelers.cfm\">Read more »</a></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<h3>K-12 Physics Master Teacher Leader Taskforce: Apply by June 30!</h3>\n<p class=\"date\">Jun 06 2016</p>\n<div class=\"contents\">\n<p>This month, the AAPT announces plans to create a Physics Master Teacher Leader (PhysicsMTL) Taskforce. This one-year recognition and leadership opportunity is a call to bring together the \"best of best\" of K-12 teachers of physics to create a new set of aspirational and coherent professional development and leadership models for the K-12 physics education community. Apply to <a href=\"http://goo.gl/forms/ZUYZeIBM8sHVzrHI3\">http://goo.gl/forms/ZUYZeIBM8sHVzrHI3</a>. He was a meticulous scholar, a wise counselor, a tireless advocate for human rights and academic freedom, and a pillar of the international particle physics community. His theoretical research was characterized by uncommon insight and a deep engagement with experiment.</p> <p>For Jackson's brief memoir click on the \"Read more\" link below. AAPT's obituary for Jackson can be found at our <a href=\"http://aapt.org/Membership/memoriam.cfm\">In Memoriam</a> page.</p>\n</div>\n<p class=\"readmore\"><a href=\"http://www.annualreviews.org/doi/pdf/10.1146/annurev.nucl.49.1.1\">Read more »</a></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<h3>AAPT Announces the 2016 U.S. Physics Team</h3>\n<p class=\"date\">May 23 2016</p>\n<div class=\"contents\">\n<p>America's brightest emerging physicists will arrive at Physics Boot Camp this week. class=\"date\">May 22 2015</p>\n<div class=\"contents\">\n<p>Super Balls are toys beloved by children because of their extraordinary ability to bounce. Physicists love them for exactly the same reason.</p><p>\"Physicists love it because it has interesting physical properties,\" said Rod Cross, retired professor of physics at the University of Sydney in Australia, whose latest paper on Super Balls appears in the <a href=\"http://scitation.aip.org/content/aapt/journal/ajp/83/3/10.1119/1.4898312\"><i>American Journal of Physics</i></a>. His research also demonstrated the odd way all balls roll.</p>\n</div>\n<p class=\"readmore\"><a href=\"http://www.insidescience.org/content/why-physicists-love-super-balls/2881\">Read more »</a></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<h3>Applied Physicist Robert G.W. Millie Dresselhaus, former recipient of the Oersted Medal, is among the diverse group of recipients who are recognized for making \"extraordinary contributions to our country and the world.\" Millie will be honored in a White House ceremony with other luminaries, including Isabel Allende, Tom Brokaw, Ethel Kennedy, Meryl Streep, and Stevie Wonder, on November 24.</p>\n</div>\n<p class=\"readmore\"><a href=\"http://www.aip.org/news/2014/millie-dresselhaus-wins-presidential-medal-freedom\">Read more »</a></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<h3>AAPT Announces the Results of the 2014 Executive Board Election</h3>\n<p class=\"date\">Nov 07 2014</p>\n<div class=\"contents\">\n<p>The AAPT membership has elected the following to serve on the AAPT Executive Board:<br>Vice President: <a href=\"http://www.aapt.org/aboutaapt/organization/George-Amann-2014-Election-Bio.cfm\">George Amann</a><br>Member at Large (TYC): <a href=\"http://www.aapt.org/aboutaapt/organization/Sherry-Savrda-2014-Election-Bio.cfm\">Sherry Savrda</a><br>Secretary: <a href=\"http://www.aapt.org/aboutaapt/organization/Christian_2014_election_bio.cfm\">Wolfgang Christian</a></p>\n</div>\n</li>\n<li>\n<h3>2015 AAPT Winter Meeting Service Awards</h3>\n<p class=\"date\">Oct 29 2014</p>\n<div class=\"contents\">\n<p>AAPT has announced that the Homer L. His work has been notable for its range, depth and impact, as well for its international scope.  Through his work Cedric Linder has helped to change the way in which physics is taught by enabling colleagues to appreciate the learning experience of students. He has influenced lives by opening up physics to many disadvantaged students, and he has added new theoretical insights and methodological approaches to the practice of physics education research.\n</p>\n<p>The full citation for Professor Linder is available (click read more below).\n</p>\n</div>\n<p class=\"readmore\"><a href=\"http://www.iupap-icpe.org/sites/default/files/ICPE/2014_citation_Linder.pdf\">Read more »</a></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<h3>High School Physics Textbooks, Resources and Teacher Resourcefulness</h3>\n<p class=\"date\">Aug 06 2014</p>\n<div class=\"contents\">\n<p>AIP has just released the results from the 2012-13 Nationwide Survey of High School Physics Teachers.</p>\n</div>\n<p class=\"readmore\"><a href=\" http://www.aip.org/statistics/reports/high-school-physics-textbooks-resources-and-teacher-resourcefulness\">Read more »</a></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<h3>2014 U.S. Physics Team Scores Five Medals in Astana, Kazakhstan</h3>\n<p class=\"date\">Jul 21 2014</p>\n<div class=\"contents\">\n<p>The top U.S. physics students scored three gold medals and two silver medals at the 45th International Physics Olympiad (IPHO), held this year from July 13 - 21 in Astana, Kazakhstan where the best high school physics students from 86 countries competed.</p>\n</div>\n<p class=\"readmore\"><a href=\"http://www.aapt.org/aboutaapt/2014-US-Physics-Team-Scores-Five-Medals.cfm\">Read more »</a></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<h3>US Physics Team is at IPHO 2014</h3>\n<p class=\"date\">Jul 15 2014</p>\n<div class=\"contents\">\n<p>Follow the team on Flickr.</p>\n</div>\n<p class=\"readmore\"><a href=\"https://www.flickr.com/photos/physicsteachers\">Read more »</a></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<h3>Journal Serivce Impact Notice</h3>\n<p class=\"date\">Jun 30 2014</p>\n<div class=\"contents\">\n<p>During the period July1-10, AIPP will be migrating to a new service provider. The development of these standards is the first step towards more uniform standards in science. The public will only have three weeks to provide feedback on the NGSS.\nAchieve has a formal <a href=\"https://achieve.qualtrics.com/SE/?SID=SV_9tYcVBMRgyCbcLq\" target=\"_blank\">survey</a> to complete by June 1st . If you are interested in preparing your responses before actually going to the survey, a PDF version of the survey is <a href=\"http://www.nextgenscience.org/sites/ngss/files/May_Release_Public_Survey_final.pdf\" target=\"_blank\">available</a>.\nThe survey is arranged so that you can provide feedback on all aspects of the standards - science &amp; engineering practices, crosscutting concepts, as well as core disciplinary content - and also on different grades and grade bands.</p>\n</div>\n</li>\n<li>\n<h3>2012 AAPT Summer Meeting</h3>\n<p class=\"date\">May 09 2012</p>\n<div class=\"contents\">\n<p>AAPT is pleased to announce that registration for the 2012 AAPT Summer Meeting in Philadelphia, PA is now open. McGraw, Jr. Prize in Education.</a>.\n</p><h2> </h2>\nThe 2011 winners are being honored for pioneering digital education approaches. As part of the award Beichner collaborated with the other prize winners, Mitchel Resnick and Julie Young, to author a <a href=\"http://mcgraw-hillresearchfoundation.org/wp-content/uploads/2011/09/White-Paper-Technology-and-the-Human-Connection.pdf\">white paper </a>citing how education technology can cultivate human connections. With an introduction by Dr. Steven Paine, vice president of CTB/McGraw-Hill and the former State Superintendent of Schools in West Virginia, the paper draws on the collective insights and perspectives of the Prize winners spanning across elementary, secondary and post-secondary education.<p></p>\n</div>\n</li>\n<li>\n<h3>9/11 from a Science Perspective</h3>\n<p class=\"date\">Sep 09 2011</p>\n<div class=\"contents\">\n<p>A few months after September 11, 2001 the Director of the National Science Foundation, Rita Colwell, delivered a speech to the Woodrow Wilson International Center for Scholars entitled <i>\"Science: Before and After September 11\"</i>.</p>\n</div>\n<p class=\"readmore\"><a href=\"http://www.nsf.gov/news/speeches/colwell/rc011107wodrowilson.htm\">Read more »</a></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<h3>AAPT National Election</h3>\n<p class=\"date\">Sep 06 2011</p>\n<div class=\"contents\">\n<p>The election of officers for Executive Board service beginning in 2012 will begin on September 19, 2011. The Olympiad, held July 10-17, was sponsored by the Promotion of Academic Olympiads and Development of Science Education Foundation (POSN), under the patronage of Her Royal Highness Princess Galyani Vadhana Krom Luang Naradhiwas Rajanagarindra, and Chulalongkorn University (CU), in Bangkok, Thailand.</p>\n</div>\n<p class=\"readmore\"><a href=\"http://aapt.org/physicsteam/2011/2011-US-Physics-Team-Scores-Two-Gold-and-3-Silver-Medals.cfm\">Read more »</a></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<h3>Intersociety Letter to Key Lawmakers</h3>\n<p class=\"date\">Jul 13 2011</p>\n<div class=\"contents\">\n<p>AAPT joined over 140 organizations and universities in signing a AAAS letter that went to the Chairman and Ranking Member of the House Appropriations Committee urging \"strong support for the federal research and development budget of the National Science Foundation (NSF), and its mission to advance research across a broad spectrum of disciplines, research that has fueled American economic growth for decades.\"  Copies were also sent to all members of the House Appropriations Committee.</p>\n<p>See the <a href=\"http://www.aaas.org/spp/cstc/docs/11-07-11nsf_letter.pdf\">letter</a> and the\n<a href=\"http://www.aaas.org/news/releases/2011/0711nsf_letter.shtml\">story.</a></p>\n</div>\n</li>\n<li>\n<h3>42nd International Physics Olympiad</h3>\n<p class=\"date\">Jul 10 2011</p>\n<div class=\"contents\">\n<p>The US Physics Team is in Thailand at the International Physics Olympiad.
